 According to officials of the space station, the highest-weight earth-monitoring 'telenos' satellite among the satellites sent with the rocket is 400 kg

 mitti ke adhyayan ke vigyaan ko mrudaa vigyaan yaneepadologikaha jaataa he
 The Indian Council of Agricultural Research has divided the soil of India into 8 classes
 1
 Alluvial soil> This soil is found on about 22% of the area of india
 >yah nadiyon dwaara laayi gayi mitti he
 This soil is rich in potash, but lacks nitrogen, phosphorus and humus
 >yah mitti 2 prakaar kii hoti he:-1
 Bangar 2
 khadar(khadar)>puraani jalodh mitti ko bangar or nayi jalodh mitti ko khadar kaha jaataa he
 > Alluvial soil is considered very good from the point of view of fertility
 isamen dhan, genhu, makka, tilhan, dalhan aadi fasalein ugaai jaati hai
 2
 kaali mitti (blike soil)> iskaa nirmaan besalt chattaanon ke tuutane-footne se hota he
 It is rich in iron, lime, aluminum starch and magnesium
 > is mitti kaa kaala rang titenepheras magnetic or jeevansh (humas) kii upasthiti ke kaaran hota he
 > This soil is also known as Regur soil
 > kaali mitti kapaas kii kheti ke liye sabase zyada upyukt hoti he isliye ise kaali kapaas kii mitti yani blike coton soil bhi kaha jaataa he
 > Other crops include wheat, jowar, millet etc
 3
 Red soil> It is formed due to dissolution and dissolution of the riveted and metamorphic rocks due to water-air change
 > is mitti main silica or aayran bahulata hoti he
 > The red color of red clay is due to the presence of iron oxide, but it appears yellow in hydrated form
 > yah amleey prakruti kii mitti hoti he
 It lacks nitrogen, phosphorus and humus
 > yah mitti urvartaa viheen banjar bhoomi ke rup main pai jaati he
 > Cotton, wheat, pulses and coarse grains are cultivated in this soil
 > bharat menyah mitti andhra pradesh or madhya pradesh ke purvi bhaag, chotanagpur ke pathari kshetra, pashchim bengal ke uttari pashchim jilon, meghalaya kii gaaro khaasi or jayantiya ke pahari kshetron, nagaland, rajasthan main aravali ke purvi kshetra, maharashtra, tamilnadu or karnataka ke kuch bhaagon main pai jaati he
 > Fertility of red soil can be increased by using lime
 4
 Laterite Soil> It is formed under specific conditions resulting from gradual changes in humidity and dryness of monsoon climate
 >isamen aayran or silica kii bahulata hoti he
 > This soil, formed from the breakage of rocks, is classified as deep red laterite, white laterite and subterranean aquifer laterite:> deep red laterite, which contains a majority of iron oxide and potash
 isaki urvartaa kam hoti he lekin nichle bhaag main kuch kheti kii ja sakati he> safed lateritaiski urvartaa sabase kam hoti he or keolin ke kaaran iskaa rang safed hota he
 > Underground aquatic laterite This soil is very fertile as iron oxide dissolves with water during rainy season
